| <span data-ttu-id="08fcf-1653">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08fcf-1653">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="08fcf-1654">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="08fcf-1654">Value</span></span> |
